# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/cilium--v1.16.5`

# Task: Implement PolicyQuotaController for Cilium

## Objective
Create a `PolicyQuotaController` in Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the
number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.

## Requirements

1. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`** with:
   - `PolicyQuotaController` struct that watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
   - `NewPolicyQuotaController(client, informer, maxPerNamespace int)` constructor
   - `Run(ctx context.Context)` method implementing the controller loop
   - Per-namespace counting using a thread-safe map
   - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error` method that returns error if quota exceeded

2. **Create CRD type** `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`:
   - `CiliumPolicyQuota` struct with `Spec.MaxPoliciesPerNamespace` field
   - Follow existing Cilium CRD patterns (DeepCopy, runtime.Object)

3. **Create `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`** with tests

4. **Follow Cilium patterns**:
   - Use `hive` dependency injection framework
   - Use `resource.Resource[T]` for watching K8s resources
   - Use `logfields` for structured logging

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/policy/k8s/watcher.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy watcher pattern
- `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_cnp.go` — CiliumNetworkPolicy CRD type
- `operator/pkg/ciliumenvoyconfig/` — controller using hive pattern
- `pkg/k8s/resource/resource.go` — resource watching framework

## Success Criteria
- PolicyQuotaController struct with Run method exists
- CheckQuota method performs namespace counting
- CiliumPolicyQuota CRD type exists
- Uses Cilium's hive/resource patterns
- Test file exists with test functions

100-usertool_resultRead
    60→	}
    61→	return nil
    62→}
    63→
    64→// Run starts the policy quota controller loop. It watches CiliumNetworkPolicy
    65→// resources and maintains per-namespace counts to enforce quotas.
    66→func (p *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {
    67→	p.log.Info("Starting PolicyQuotaController")
    68→
    69→	events := p.cnpResource.Events(ctx)
    70→	for {
    71→		select {
    72→		case <-ctx.Done():
    73→			p.log.Info("PolicyQuotaController stopped")
    74→			return ctx.Err()
    75→		case event, ok := <-events:
    76→			if !ok {
    77→				p.log.Info("PolicyQuotaController event channel closed")
    78→				return nil
    79→			}
    80→
    81→			var err error
    82→			switch event.Kind {
    83→			case resource.Sync:
    84→				p.log.Debug("PolicyQuotaController synced with API server")
    85→				event.Done(nil)
    86→				continue
    87→
    88→			case resource.Upsert:
    89→				err = p.handlePolicyUpsert(event.Object)
    90→
    91→			case resource.Delete:
    92→				err = p.handlePolicyDelete(event.Object)
    93→			}
    94→
    95→			event.Done(err)
    96→		}
    97→	}
    98→}
    99→

A value of 0 means unlimited.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tlogger logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tcnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlog:                   logger,\n\t\tcnpResource:           cnpResource,\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tnamespacePolicyCounts: make(map[string]int),\n\t}\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks whether creating a new policy in the given namespace\n// would exceed the per-namespace quota. Returns an error if quota would be exceeded.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif p.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil // Unlimited quota\n\t}\n\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tcurrentCount := p.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]\n\tp.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tif currentCount >= p.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"policy quota exceeded for namespace %s: current %d, max %d\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, currentCount, p.maxPerNamespace,\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// Run starts the policy quota controller loop. It watches CiliumNetworkPolicy\n// resources and maintains per-namespace counts to enforce quotas.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tp.log.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\tevents := p.cnpResource.Events(ctx)\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tp.log.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController stopped\")\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tp.log.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController event channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\tp.log.Debug(\"PolicyQuotaController synced with API server\")\n\t\t\t\tevent.Done(nil)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = p.handlePolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr = p.handlePolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// handlePolicyUpsert handles the addition or update of a CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) handlePolicyUpsert(cnp *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := cnp.GetNamespace()\n\n\tp.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer p.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tp.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace:            namespace,\n\t\tlogfields.CiliumNetworkPolicyName: cnp.GetName(),\n\t}).Debug(\"Handling policy upsert\")\n\n\tp.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]++\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// handlePolicyDelete handles the deletion of a CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) handlePolicyDelete(cnp *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := cnp.GetNamespace()\n\n\tp.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer p.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tp.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace:            namespace,\n\t\tlogfields.CiliumNetworkPolicyName: cnp.GetName(),\n\t}).Debug(\"Handling policy delete\")\n\n\tcount := p.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]\n\tif count > 0 {\n\t\tp.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]--\n\t}\n\n\t// Clean up empty entries\n\tif p.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\tdelete(p.namespacePolicyCounts, namespace)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// GetNamespacePolicyCounts returns a copy of the current per-namespace policy counts.\n// This is useful for testing and monitoring.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) GetNamespacePolicyCounts() map[string]int {\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer p.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tcounts := make(map[string]int)\n\tfor k, v := range p.namespacePolicyCounts {\n\t\tcounts[k] = v\n\t}\n\treturn counts\n}\n",

package v2

import (
	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
)

// +genclient
// +k8s:deepcopy-gen:interfaces=k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/runtime.Object
// +deepequal-gen:private-method=true
// +kubebuilder:resource:categories={cilium,ciliumpolicy},singular="ciliumpolicyquota",path="ciliumpolicyquotas",scope="Namespaced",shortName={cpq}
// +kubebuilder:printcolumn:JSONPath=".metadata.creationTimestamp",name="Age",type=date
// +kubebuilder:storageversion

// CiliumPolicyQuota defines per-namespace limits on the number of
// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources to prevent policy sprawl.
type CiliumPolicyQuota struct {
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata"`

	// Spec is the desired Cilium policy quota specification.
	Spec CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec `json:"spec,omitempty"`

	// Status is the status of the Cilium policy quota
	//
	// +deepequal-gen=false
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Optional
	Status CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus `json:"status"`
}

// +deepequal-gen=true

// CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec defines the policy quota specification.
type CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec struct {
	// MaxPoliciesPerNamespace is the maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy
	// resources allowed per namespace. A value of 0 means unlimited.
	//
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Minimum=0
	MaxPoliciesPerNamespace int `json:"maxPoliciesPerNamespace,omitempty"`

	// NamespaceSelector specifies which namespaces this quota applies to.
	// If empty, the quota applies to all namespaces.
	//
	// +kubebuilder:validation:Optional
	NamespaceSelector *metav1.LabelSelector `json:"namespaceSelector,omitempty"`
}

2. WRITE /workspace/pkg/policy/quota/controller.go
// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
// Copyright Authors of Cilium

package quota

import (
	"context"
	"fmt"
	"sync"

	"github.com/sirupsen/logrus"

	cilium_v2 "github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/k8s/resource"
	"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/logging/logfields"
)

// PolicyQuotaController enforces per-namespace limits on the number of
// CiliumNetworkPolicy resources to prevent policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.
type PolicyQuotaController struct {
	log                   logrus.FieldLogger
	cnpResource           resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
	maxPerNamespace       int
	namespacePolicyCounts map[string]int
	mu                    sync.RWMutex
}

// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.
// maxPerNamespace specifies the maximum number of CiliumNetworkPolicy resources
// allowed per namespace. A value of 0 means unlimited.
func NewPolicyQuotaController(
	logger logrus.FieldLogger,
	cnpResource resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],
	maxPerNamespace int,
) *PolicyQuotaController {
	return &PolicyQuotaController{
		log:                   logger,
		cnpResource:           cnpResource,
		maxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,
		namespacePolicyCounts: make(map[string]int),
	}
}

// CheckQuota checks whether creating a new policy in the given namespace
// would exceed the per-namespace quota. Returns an error if quota would be exceeded.
func (p *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {
	if p.maxPerNamespace == 0 {
		return nil // Unlimited quota
	}

	p.mu.RLock()
	currentCount := p.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]
	p.mu.RUnlock()

	if currentCount >= p.maxPerNamespace {
		return fmt.Errorf(
			"policy quota exceeded for namespace %s: current %d, max %d",
... (truncated)

type mockCNPResource struct {
	events chan resource.Event[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]
}

	// In a real implementation, these would be properly closed.
	// For testing, we just return the channel.
	return m.events
}

func (m *mockCNPResource) Store(ctx context.Context) (resource.Store[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy], error) {
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("not implemented in mock")
}

			namespace: "ns3",

1. **Per-Namespace Policy Counting**
   - Thread-safe map to track policy counts per namespace
   - Automatically updated on CNP create/delete events

2. **Quota Enforcement**

   - Returns descriptive error message when exceeded
   - Supports unlimited quota (maxPerNamespace = 0)

3. **Resource Watching**
   - Uses Cilium's resource.Resource pattern
   - Properly handles event lifecycle (Upsert, Delete, Sync)
   - Calls Done() on all events to maintain event stream

4. **Thread Safety**
   - RWMutex protects concurrent access to count map
   - Safe for parallel policy updates

   - Uses logrus FieldLogger for structured logging
   - Follows hive/cell dependency injection style
   - Uses resource.Resource for K8s resource watching
   - Proper SPDX license headers
